### 16. 时尚 LCD 脸机器人提示

**Author**: [Toshi](https://x.com/ToshiArte)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: en

### 40. 详细的 X 射线透明玫瑰艺术提示

**Author**: [A1-CREATE](https://x.com/a1createsh)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: ja

> 一个极其详细、结构化的提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro（通过 GeminiApp）生成一幅玫瑰的 X 射线透明艺术图像。该提示详细说明了构图、主体设计（侧重于单朵花朵的中心旋涡）、渲染模式和密度映射，旨在生成高度逼真、近乎单色但带有微妙色彩提示的图像。

![详细的 X 射线透明玫瑰艺术提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469813505_o425wy_HDR42A4asAAA8Lu.jpg)

```
meta:
  title: "バラのX線透過アート - 花弁だけで埋める単輪寄り・中心渦強調"
  concept: "ほぼ単輪のバラだけで画面を埋め尽くし、真上からの極端な超接写で中心渦を強烈に見せる、ほぼモノクロのX線ファインアート。花弁内部にだけ、ごくわずかなバラらしい色味を忍ばせる"
  language: "ja"

output:
  aspect_ratio: "4:5"
  orientation: "縦"
  resolution_intent: "高解像度"
  deliverable_type: "単輪寄り花弁充満の植物X線・微着彩"

scene:
  genre: "植物X線写真"
  subject: "バラ"
  subject_count_impression: "ほぼ単輪、周辺に断片的な花弁のみ"
  realism_level: "高"
  environment: "スタジオでの単体撮影"
  mood:
    - "静謐"
    - "官能的"
    - "精緻"
    - "緊張感"
    - "吸い込まれるような中心渦"
    - "上品な微着彩"
  background:
    type: "実質不可視"
    color: "#F3F3F1"
    texture: "なし"
    gradient: "なし"
    vignette: "なし"

composition:
  framing: "真上からの極端な超接写"
  camera_angle: "俯瞰マクロ"
  perspective: "中心渦へ吸引されるような平面的かつ密着した真上視点"
  crop_style: "極端に大胆なクロップ"
  subject_fill_ratio: "画面の97から100パーセント"
  visual_goal: "画面全体をほぼ一輪のバラの花弁層だけで埋め、中心渦の構造を圧倒的な主役として見せる"
  bouquet_layout:
    overall_shape: "単輪の巨大な花頭が画面を占有"
    center_focus: "中央やや上または中央ちょうどに巨大な花芯渦"
    bloom_distribution:
      hero_bloom:
        role: "絶対的主役のバラ"
        position: "中央付近"
        scale: "極大"
        openness: "中心は密に締まり、外周は大きくほどける"
        crop: "外周花弁の大部分が全辺でフレームアウト"
      secondary_blooms:
        count: 0
        role: "なし"
        placement: []
        openness_variation: []
      peripheral_petals:
        count_impression: "必要ならごくわずか"
        role: "単輪をさらに巨大に感じさせる外周断片"
        treatment: "別花に見えない範囲で、外周の切れた花弁片としてのみ存在"
  petal_flow:
    directionality: "極度に明確な螺旋運動"
    energy: "非常に高い"
    motion_impression: "中心渦から外へ向かって連続的に花弁が解放される"
    asymmetry: "自然で緊張感のある非対称"
  leaves_and_stems:
    visibility: "ゼロに近い"
    purpose: "原則描写しない"
    leaves:
      placement: "なし"
      crop: "なし"
      shape: "なし"
      amount: "ゼロ"
    stems:
      visibility: "ゼロ"
      arrangement: "なし"
  negative_space:
    amount: "ゼロに近い"
    purpose: "没入感の最大化"

subject_design:
  flower_species: "バラ"
  bouquet_style: "単輪寄り超拡大構成"

### 41. Vlog 风格时尚视频提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro 和 Google Veo 3.1

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，首先用于 Nano Banana Pro 生成图像，然后用于 Google Veo 3.1 生成视频。该提示描述了一个电影般的、逼真的、高质量的视频，在室内夜间拍摄，重点是一位面带温柔微笑的女性，她正准备开始录制 Vlog，讨论她的时尚要点。该提示包括具体的摄像机角度、灯光、氛围和对话。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Intimate Atmosphere]] [[Google Veo Video Generation]]

### 44. 单色动态产品摄影提示

**Author**: [Ivan](https://x.com/ai_artdirector)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张高端、极简主义的美容编辑图片：画面中，双手握持一个护肤品瓶子，采用单色调，通过运动模糊效果（重影/多重曝光）来传达动感能量，并辅以柔和、高调的影棚照明。

![单色动态产品摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469798579_4xb2jq_HDQydCnbAAAkRZK.jpg)

```
[WHAT_IT_IS] Commerce/editorial product image. Monochrome studio study of a skincare bottle held between two hands with pronounced multi-frame motion blur for kinetic, airy minimalism. [SUBJECT_SCENE] Two hands occupy the frame on a pale seamless background, positioned diagonally: the upper hand enters from the right holding a small cylindrical pump bottle near the top-left quadrant, while a second hand below reaches upward from the lower-left, fingers open as if about to receive the product. The bottle is angled slightly downward-left, label side facing camera, with a matte body and a reflective metallic pump/collar that catches bright highlights. The hands are rendered with visible multi-exposure ghosting--each hand shows several offset silhouettes trailing along the direction of motion, especially around fingertips, creating a layered flutter effect. The bottle remains comparatively stable and readable, acting as the sharp anchor amid the blur, though its edges show slight softness consistent with motion. Composition is sparse and balanced: large negative space surrounds the central hand/product cluster, and the diagonal hand positions create a gentle "handoff" narrative. Focus is shallow-to-moderate but controlled so the product stays the visual priority while the ghosting conveys movement rather than defocus. [BACKGROUND] Clean pale gray/white seamless with no horizon line, reading as a minimal studio field. [LIGHTING_EFFECTS] Bright, diffused high-key lighting produces smooth tonal gradients on skin and the bottle body, with minimal harsh shadow edges. The metallic pump reflects a tight highlight band, indicating a slightly harder specular component within an otherwise soft setup. Motion effects read as long-exposure or composited frame trails: semi-transparent duplicates of the hands stack with decreasing opacity, creating soft-edged blur that is most intense at the fingertips and less pronounced near the wrists. Shadows are faint and washed, suggesting strong fill and a background pushed toward white; any contact shadowing is reduced to soft gray haze beneath the hands. The overall contrast is moderate, with skin texture subtly visible but simplified by the monochrome treatment and diffusion. No heavy bloom; instead the "airiness" comes from high-key exposure and the layered motion trails. [IMAGE_STYLE] Minimalist, high-end beauty editorial--monochrome palette, negative space, and kinetic motion-blur compositing to imply sensorial application/ritual. Designed to feel premium and modern, translating product handling into an abstract, graphic gesture.
```

[[High Key Lighting]] [[Motion Blur Effect]] [[Beauty Product Photography]]

### 54. Nano Banana Pro 图像提示解构的系统提示

**Author**: [jeenie](https://x.com/jinwen189431)  **Date**: 2026-03-12  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个系统提示，旨在指导 Nano Banana Pro（一个图像生成模型）充当专业的图像提示解构专家。任务是分析图像并输出一个中文提示，该提示可用于重新生成图像，优先考虑文本内容 (P0) 和视觉细节 (P1)。这是一个用于生成其他提示的元提示，而不是直接的图像生成提示。

![Nano Banana Pro 图像提示解构的系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383503371_wptd0o_HDM9MF0bgAA7_Bd.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 图像提示解构的系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383503421_nzewwz_HDM9Ng4bQAA6OOv.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 图像提示解构的系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383503454_y4qdk9_HDM9M6Mb0AAkEBG.jpg)

```

### 59. Vlog 风格时尚视频提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-12  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成图像，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 制作视频。该提示描述了一个稳定、固定机位的女性镜头，用于营造真实、亲密的视频博客时刻，重点是自然光线、放松的表情和特定的对话。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Google Veo Video Generation]]

### 65. Nano Banana 的角色参考表提示词

**Author**: [Aimi Kōda](https://x.com/aimikoda)  **Date**: 2026-03-12  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的提示，用于生成一位优雅年轻女性的专业角色参考表，其中包含主体细节、服装、电影级真实感风格以及包括多个视角和一致解剖结构在内的布局要求。

![Nano Banana 的角色参考表提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383491103_hhni09_HDLRqnxXoAAp4Zn.jpg)
![Nano Banana 的角色参考表提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383491140_06nvbr_HDLRrk4XsAAL6VE.jpg)

```
[SUBJECT] = {argument name="subject description" default="elegant attractive young woman with blonde bob hair, large almond-shaped blue eyes, narrow nose, high cheekbones and delicate angular facial structure"}
[OUTFIT] = {argument name="outfit description" default="A dark charcoal or muted navy thin knit top paired with a long, softly draped cardigan or a simple coat made from a gentle textured fabric. The look is completed with straight-cut dark trousers or a matte fabric skirt. Accessories are kept minimal, such as small earrings and a delicate thin ring. The hair appears slightly tousled and natural, avoiding an overly polished or carefully styled look."}
[OUTPUT_STYLE] = cinematic realism.

Make a professional character reference sheet of [SUBJECT] in [OUTPUT_STYLE] in 16:9 aspect ratio. Use a full-frame camera with a 50mm lens when rendering photographic styles. Set a plain pure white background with no environment elements. Place a large full-body front view of [SUBJECT] standing upright in a neutral pose on the left side of the sheet. Place two smaller turnaround views in the upper right section. Show a full-body back view standing upright in the same neutral pose. Show a full-body left side profile standing upright in the same neutral pose. Place one dynamic full-body action pose of [SUBJECT] in the middle right section. Place a side profile portrait close-up of [SUBJECT] in the lower right section. Show [SUBJECT] wearing [OUTFIT] consistently across all views. Keep anatomy, proportions, outfit details and hairstyle perfectly consistent across all views. Use soft studio key light from front-left. Use subtle fill light from front-right. Use a soft rim light from behind for silhouette separation. Ensure clarity, accuracy, and professional finish.
```

[{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}]

[{argument name="Product Type" default="PRODUCT TYPE"}] (Clothing / Food / Automotive / Tech).

Goal: Generate a professional "scrapbook" style collage poster for [{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}] centered around a [{argument name="Product Type" default="PRODUCT TYPE"}].

1. HERO PRODUCT (BOTTOM FOCUS)

- Object: A high-definition, realistic 3D render of a [{argument name="Product Type" default="PRODUCT TYPE"}] by [{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}] at the bottom center.

- Placement: Slightly angled to show depth, with soft realistic contact shadows on a plain off-white floor.

2. THE MULTI-LAYERED COLLAGE STACK

- Photos: A vertical stack of overlapping photos with RAGGED, TORN paper edges rising above the product.

- Content: Photos should show [{argument name="Product Type" default="PRODUCT TYPE"}] in use, lifestyle shots related to [{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}], and close-ups of specific details.

- Materials: Physical swatches of textures related to [{argument name="Product Type" default="PRODUCT TYPE"}] (e.g., leather/fabric for clothing, metal/carbon for cars, organic ingredients for food). Include visible raw edges and stitching.

- Fasteners: Use strips of semi-transparent masking tape and black duct tape with the "[{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}]" logo printed in white to "hold" the pieces together.

3. GRAPHIC OVERLAYS & STAMPS

- Stamp: A black, distressed ink stamp or seal near the hero product with text: "AUTHENTIC QUALITY // SUSTAINABLE CHOICE".

- Typography: Small, clean sans-serif and typewriter-style text blocks describing the heritage of [{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}] placed at the bottom.

- Logo: The primary "[{argument name="Brand Name" default="BRAND NAME"}]" logo centered at the very bottom in a minimalist font.

4. STYLE & ATMOSPHERE

- Aesthetic: Industrial DIY, workshop moodboard, high-end editorial collage.

- Lighting: Bright, studio high-key lighting with soft, multi-layered shadows between the paper scraps and textures.

- Quality: 8K resolution, macro detail on paper grain, fabric fibers, and tape adhesive.
```

The chattering teeth stand inside an overflowing toy box made of painted wood, its interior cluttered with colorful toys—tiny cars, sparkling plastic jewelry, wrapped candies, rubber balls, and scattered trinkets—some spilling over the edge. Soft, diffused lighting creates gentle shadows and a cozy, nostalgic atmosphere, with a shallow depth of field subtly blurring the background toys to keep the focus on the animated chattering teeth and feet.
```

### 102. Nano Banana/Gemini 图像生成基准提示

**Author**: [相武 辰昌](https://x.com/AimuMe)  **Date**: 2026-03-09  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细、多方面的基准测试提示，旨在通过检查文本一致性、解剖学准确性、材质渲染、空间光照以及提示遵循/属性分离这五个特定的“难点”，来测试 Nano Banana/Gemini 等图像生成模型的极限。

![Nano Banana/Gemini 图像生成基准提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124352662_gftxiv_HC_37MwaMAInGId.jpg)
![Nano Banana/Gemini 图像生成基准提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124352769_oqsj5v_HC_4HEFaMAM08dE.jpg)
![Nano Banana/Gemini 图像生成基准提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124353053_nn8xti_HC_4IKJaAAAqs6-.jpg)

```
このプロンプトでチェックすべき「5つの難所」
この1枚の画像が生成されたら、以下のポイントを拡大して確認してみてください。

・テキストの整合性 (AI EVOLUTION 2026)
段ボールのサインに書かれた文字が、スペルミスなく、かつ「手書き風」の質感を保ちつつ正しくレンダリングされているか。

・解剖学的正確性と相互作用
老人の「10本の指」が、ガラスの蝶という壊れやすい物体を自然に保持しているか。指が背景に溶けたり、数が狂ったりしていないか。

・質感の描き分け（マテリアル・ミックス）
「老人の肌（シワ）」「クロームメッキ（鏡面）」「ガラス（透過）」「ベルベット（起毛）」「液体（湯気）」という、反射率や透過率が全く異なる素材が、同一の光源下で矛盾なく描かれているか。

・空間と光の計算（レイトレーシング的理解）
アンドロイドの青い発光が、老人のメガネや周囲の金属に正しく反射しているか。複数の光源による影が矛盾していないか。

・プロンプト追従性と属性の分離
「左に老人」「右にアンドロイド」という配置が守られているか。「赤いベルベット」の色がアンドロイドの肌に移ったり、老人の服が青くなったりする「色移り（Color Bleeding）」が起きていないか。
```

[[Anatomical Accuracy]]

---

### 103. 电影级水下潜水场景

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2026-03-09  **Language**: en

> 为 Gemini Nano Banana 生成电影般水下场景的高度详细提示。角色（基于参考）处于潜水中期，正向下方的镜头俯冲。提示中指定了极端的透视畸变（超广角镜头）、动态动作（气泡、飘逸的头发）以及环境细节（清澈的热带水域、体积感阳光束）。

![电影级水下潜水场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124340406_c25yyo_HC_UFNCaMAEuTZb.jpg)

```
A cinematic underwater scene captured from a submerged camera deep in a crystal-clear ocean.
The reference character has just jumped into the water and is rapidly diving downward toward the camera.
Perspective & Camera
The camera is positioned underwater, looking sharply upward toward the ocean surface from below.
Extreme perspective pressure: the character’s face is very close to the lens and dominates the foreground, appearing large and powerful, while the body rapidly recedes into depth due to perspective distortion.
Shot with an ultra-wide 18–20mm underwater lens.
The character’s head sits slightly off-center, breaking symmetry.
The torso and legs stretch upward into the distance toward the bright water surface above.
Action
The character is mid-dive, cutting through the water with speed and momentum.
Hair, clothing, or accessories flow upward due to the downward motion.
Streams of bubbles explode around the character’s face and shoulders as they plunge deeper.
Environment
The water is extremely clear tropical ocean water with deep blue gradients.
Sunlight rays penetrate the surface above, creating volumetric beams through the water.
Schools of small fish swim around the scene, some crossing in front of the lens.
Particles, tiny bubbles, and floating plankton create depth layers in the water.
Depth of Field
The character’s face is razor sharp in the focal plane.
The body progressively softens into blur as it stretches toward the surface.
Fish close to the camera appear slightly blurred due to motion and shallow depth of field.
Lighting
Natural sunlight from the surface above creates strong top lighting and shimmering caustic patterns.
Subtle rim highlights trace the edges of the character’s face and shoulders through the water.
Emotion & Energy
Dynamic, cinematic, high-energy moment of descent.
The viewer feels like they are waiting in the depths as the character rapidly approaches.
Color grade
Rich ocean blues and turquoise tones with bright white highlights from the surface light.
ar 16:9
```

[[Face Reference Photography]] [[Underwater Photography]]

### 106. 动物练习人类技能图片生成模板

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-03-09  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana 设计的复杂多步骤提示模板，用于生成动物进行人类活动的逼真、坦率的训练瞬间，例如猫练习空手道或狗举重。该提示包含技能转移、场景容器、动作、真实性限制和视觉语法等方面的详细说明。

```
<instruction>   Do this for [Animal / Creature / Pet] practicing [Human Skill / Martial Art / Discipline]:  

1. Skill Transfer: 
Input A is an animal or creature.
Input B is a human discipline, martial art, craft, sport, or skill.

Analyze both inputs and infer:

Species Motion Traits: the natural posture, balance, limb movement, paw/wing/claw use, and body proportions of Input A.

Discipline Mechanics: the essential movement or technique associated with Input B (stance, strike, block, craft motion, or tool use).

Training Interaction: determine how a human trainer, instructor, or environment would realistically guide or test the skill.

Scale & Equipment: infer the correct training props, uniforms, or equipment sized appropriately for the animal.

2. Container 
Goal: a believable practice or training scene.

The environment should be the natural location where the discipline would occur:

dojo, gym, workshop, field, training hall, studio, kitchen station, laboratory bench, etc.

The environment should contain recognizable training objects or equipment relevant to Input B.

3. Scene 

Input A actively performs the discipline in a recognizable stance or action.

A trainer, instructor, or observer may assist by holding equipment, guiding posture, or presenting a challenge (such as a target or object).

The moment should capture the key action of the skill: striking, crafting, balancing, lifting, cutting, shaping, blocking, or demonstrating technique.

4. Realism Constraint:

preserve realistic anatomy of Input A (fur patterns, whiskers, paws, tail movement, posture).

any clothing or gear must support the activity rather than dominate the scene (training belt, small uniform, gloves, apron, etc.).

tools and objects must be physically scaled so the action feels believable.

5. Visual Syntax

Camera: candid mid-range shot like a paused video frame or training moment

Lighting: natural indoor lighting or soft gym lighting

Detail: realistic fur, equipment textures, and environmental details

Mood: playful but believable, skill demonstration moment

6. Flexibility Constraint:
This should work for any combination such as:

cat practicing karate

dog lifting weights

raccoon woodworking

bird painting

rabbit gardening

The system must infer correct props, stance, and environment from the variable inputs without hardcoding specific animals or disciplines.

Output: ONE image, vertical or square aspect ratio, realistic candid training moment of an animal performing a human discipline with believable environment and props.
</instruction>
```

[[Candid Snapshot]] [[Anthropomorphic Animal]] [[Creative Concept Photography]]

### 107. 异想天开的单色朋克浮动微缩立体模型生成器（副本）

**Author**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent)  **Date**: 2026-03-09  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana 2 设计的高度复杂、结构化的提示模板，旨在生成一个基于程序朋克美学的异想天开的漂浮微缩立体模型。它包含广泛的变量指南和用于场景结构、道具、建筑和氛围的程序生成层。

![异想天开的单色朋克浮动微缩立体模型生成器（副本）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124347887_hsmjta_HC-ZF8baoAA7o8Q.jpg)

```
WHIMSICAL MONO-PUNK FLOATING MINIATURE DIORAMA PROMPT
(Automatic Background Optimization, Smart Micro-Detail System, Procedural Activity Layer, Natural Irregularity Layer, Atmospheric Depth Layer, Procedural Scene Generator, Procedural Prop Generator, Procedural Architecture Generator, Procedural Lighting & Atmosphere Generator, Procedural Character & Population Generator, Procedural Diorama Base Generator)

VARIABLE GUIDE
GLOBAL_COMPLEXITY = Possible values: 'low','medium','high','ultra'. Controls density of buildings, props, characters, and environmental detail. If blank choose randomly between 'medium' and 'high'.
PUNK_STYLE = 
If PUNK_STYLE is empty, then one style is randomly selected from LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES, otherwise what is in the PUNK_STYLE variable is chosen
LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES = Steampunk, Dieselpunk, Atompunk, Cyberpunk, Biopunk, Nanopunk, Solarpunk, Decopunk, Clockpunk, Coalpunk, Raypunk, Stonepunk, Sailpunk, Cassettepunk, Teslapunk, Mythpunk, Sandalpunk, Oceanpunk, Frostpunk, Junglepunk, Desertpunk, Gothicpunk, Ironpunk, Crystalpunk, Rustpunk, Vaporwavepunk, Neonpunk, Skypunk, Aquapunk, Arborpunk, Astropunk, QuantumPunk, Mechanopunk, Technopunk, Retrocomputingpunk, Cattlepunk, Hopepunk
SUBSTYLE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from PUNK_STYLE.
TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer from PUNK_STYLE.
ENVIRONMENT = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from active layers.
CULTURE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer culturally appropriate framework.
PROCEDURAL_SCENE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_PROP_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_ARCHITECTURE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_LIGHTING_ATMOSPHERE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_CHARACTER_POPULATION_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_DIORAMA_BASE_GENERATOR = 'on'
FOCAL_INTEREST_LAYER = off
MATERIAL_COHESION_LAYER = 'on'
VISUAL_CLARITY_OPTIMIZER = 'on'
MICRO_LIFE_LAYER = 'on'
COMPOSITION_ENGINE = 'on'
EDGE_DEFINITION_LAYER = 'on'
COLOR_HARMONY_LAYER = 'on'
DIORAMA_CRAFTSMANSHIP_LAYER = 'on'

PSG LAYER
Implement only if PROCEDURAL_SCENE_GENERATOR='on'. Generate core scene structure using:
LANDSCAPE_STRUCTURE (floating island, cliff terraces, canyon basin, harbor cove, forest clearing, mountain ridge, giant tree canopy, desert oasis, ice shelf, volcanic ridge)
SETTLEMENT_TYPE (village, harbor town, trading port, monastery complex, research outpost, fortress town, sky dock, industrial district, hidden enclave)
INFRASTRUCTURE_ELEMENTS (bridges, windmills, rail lines, cable lifts, aqueducts, airship docks, solar arrays, reactor towers, waterwheels)
CIVILIAN_ACTIVITY (market trading, fishing, cargo loading, harvesting, machine repair, patrol movement, festival gathering, workshop crafting)
MICRO_NARRATIVE (delivery arrival, festival beginning, storm approaching, caravan arrival, wildlife encoun
```

### 112. 日本女学生镜中自拍，面部隐藏

ENVIRONMENT = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from active layers.
CULTURE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer culturally appropriate framework.

The entire free-standing structure must be completely visible with negative space around it against a simple background. The aspect ratio is 3:4.  

Directive 2: The Main Structure (Strict Constraints) 
Render the image in the style of ART_STYLE. The central object is a highly detailed, permanently open-front curio display structure. It must not possess doors, hinges, or door frames of any kind. The exterior is constructed from CUPBOARD_BASE_MATERIAL and detailed with ORNAMENTATION_STYLE. The interior back wall is lined with CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL, and the individual shelves are made of RACK_MATERIAL.  

Directive 3: The Miniature Dioramas & Figures 

The structure houses a cohesive detailed miniature world divided across three shelves, adhering to the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME. Crucially, each shelf must contain miniature figures engaged in a specific narrative action. Let there be a high density of structures, props, characters. Let the detail of environment, architecture and props be high.

### 133. Nano Banana 2 提示词失败与比较

**Author**: [MIKAI](https://x.com/CD_Bana)  **Date**: 2026-03-08  **Language**: zh

> 一位用户分享了一个详细的图像生成提示词，但 nano-banana-pro 2 未能处理，尽管该提示词没有明显的违规内容。随后，该用户比较了其他模型（豆包、ChatGPT 和 Grok）使用相同提示词生成的结果。

![Nano Banana 2 提示词失败与比较](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773038349371_sx4l1u_HC5VAb4a8AANoku.jpg)

**Author**: [Yagasaki, 葛城](https://x.com/Yagasaki7K)  **Date**: 2026-03-08  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro，以一个人的照片作为身份参考，创作一张极简电影风格的时尚社论工作室肖像。它指定了构图、姿势、服装（黑色吸烟夹克）、戏剧性的高对比度照明，以及一个带有微妙发光光晕效果的纯黑色背景。

![极简电影感时尚专题影棚肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773038329655_owrpzb_HC2U5wcW0AA-DKP.jpg)

```
Using a person's photo as the identity reference, create a minimalist cinematic fashion-editorial studio portrait. Vertical 4:5, mid-torso to head framing with generous negative space above, subject slightly left of center.

Pose: shoulders angled 3/4, head turned back toward camera, chin slightly lifted. Expression calm, cool, slightly aloof, eyes relaxed and focused.

Wardrobe: {argument name="wardrobe" default="black smoking (tuxedo jacket)"}, no logos, no jewelry.

Lighting: dramatic high-contrast studio lighting. A strong neutral key light from camera-right/front-right sculpting the face and coat, deep falloff into shadow on the far side, with a very subtle low-intensity soft fill from camera-left.

Background: completely black studio environment. Behind the subject’s head, a soft diffused backlight creating a subtle glowing halo with cinematic bloom, not a solid circle. The light softly radiates outward and gradually dissolves into pure black (#000000), creating a gentle atmospheric glow around the silhouette. No visible light source, no hard edges, no textures.

Optics: 85mm portrait look, f/2–f/2.8 shallow depth of field (eyes tack sharp, background creamy), pronounced highlight bloom, soft halation around the backlight, smooth cinematic contrast, subtle film grain, crisp micro-texture in fabric weave, controlled natural skin texture.

No text, no watermark. Editorial, modern, high-detail, cinematic composition, ultra-realistic textures, professional fashion photography style.
```

      "preserve_facial_features": true
    },

      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,

        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin",
        "outer_border": "none",
        "panel_consistency": "very_high"

    },

**Author**: [timedoctor.eth](https://x.com/timedoctor_nft)  **Date**: 2026-03-07  **Language**: en

> 一个高度复杂且细节丰富的 JSON 提示，用于生成名为“结晶的忧郁”的电影级超现实肖像。它描述了一位身着融化冰晶制成的服装的主人公，置身于一个杂乱的“低温玻璃吹制工坊”中，超写实地聚焦于凝结水珠和霜冻的纹理。它还指定了情绪化的体积光（月光作为主光）和技术相机设置（哈苏 H6D-100c，80mm f/1.9 镜头），以实现编辑级的超现实主义效果。

```
{
  "vibe_title_en": "Crystallized Melancholy",
  "master_prompt": "Cinematic surreal portrait of The Protagonist captured in a dense, cluttered 'Cryogenic Glass-Blower's Workshop.' The subject is framed in a tight profile, head tilted upward in a state of frozen serenity, mirroring the composition of an ice queen but grounded in tactile reality. The environment is overwhelmingly busy and textured: shelves overflowing with shattered glass shards, hanging icicles that look like stalactites, frosted vintage tools, and suspended botanical specimens encased in solid blocks of ice. The subject wears a surreal, avant-garde garment made entirely of jagged, melting ice shards and translucent fiber-optics that mimic frost, appearing heavy and wet against the skin. Hyper-realistic details focus on the condensation on the skin, individual snowflakes caught in the eyelashes, and the refraction of blue light through the clutter. Shot on a {argument name="camera model" default="Hasselblad H6D-100c"} with an {argument name="lens aperture" default="80mm f/1.9"} lens to achieve a razor-thin depth of field, blurring the chaotic background into a bokeh of cool blues and silvers. Lighting is moody and volumetric, with a 'moonlight' key light creating harsh, dramatic shadows (Chiaroscuro) and rim lighting accentuating the frost textures. Analog film simulation of Fujifilm Pro 400H with visible grain to ground the surrealism in physical photography. NO neon, NO digital art style.",
